In literary terms, parody is also known as the parody of the parodies, an imitation of the imitation, or the imitation of the parody. In popular parlance, the term can be used to describe an artistic or cultural work that is meant to be both original and funny and to the point. Parody has been around since ancient times; however, with the advent of new mediums that have developed since then, the word \'parody\' is more often than not used to denote a comedic or witty piece or series of jokes.\\\\n\\\\nWith the new mediums of the web, there are more opportunities for parodies to come up online and more opportunities for people to share them. On the web, parodies are often posted on forums or blogs or placed in discussion groups, on social networking sites such as Facebook and Twitter, on message boards or news portals, and more. They can be shared and commented upon through websites like Facebook, where parodies are tagged and they have their own page with a description and a link back to the original website or blog. VIDEO: LL COOL J GOT THE RONA | CORONAVIRUS PARODY\\"},\\"description\\":{\\"simpleText\\":\\"A parody often called humor, satire, parody, an imitation, a lampoon, or a funny take-down, is usually a short, dramatic work that is made to poke fun at and mock-up the subject of original work, its author, style, or any other intended target. In literary terms, parody is also known as the parody of the parodies, an imitation of the imitation, or the imitation of the parody. In popular parlance, the term can be used to describe an artistic or cultural work that is meant to be both original and funny and to the point. Parody has been around since ancient times; however, with the advent of new mediums that have developed since then, the word \'parody\' is more often than not used to denote a comedic or witty piece or series of jokes.\\\\n\\\\nWith the new mediums of the web, there are more opportunities for parodies to come up online and more opportunities for people to share them. On the web, parodies are often posted on forums or blogs or placed in discussion groups, on social networking sites such as Facebook and Twitter, on message boards or news portals, and more. They can be shared and commented upon through websites like Facebook, where parodies are tagged and they have their own page with a description and a link back to the original website or blog. Similarly, there are web pages, websites, chat rooms, and email groups dedicated solely to parodying particular genres of art, literature, film, television, or music.\\\\n\\\\nThere are a few things that a person can do in order to make a parody website that looks good and will attract a lot of visitors who may be interested in the parodic material. One of the first things that a person must do is to draw up an eye-catching site design and create an interesting title for it. The content of a parody website should be able to stand out and grab the attention of the viewer; the website should not necessarily be a one-dimensional comedy piece, but rather it should be able to deliver information about the subject matter.\\\\n\\\\nIn terms of web pages, the content should be original, informative, witty, yet funny, and informative. Some web pages have the name of the author attached to them and others do not. If the name of the author is used on the website, it would not only be embarrassing to some readers; it could also give offense to the author of the original work. {if he or she was to become a target of the web pages which have the name on them. So, the name of the author of the website should not be on the website, and if the name is not included on the website, then it can be a good idea to include a link back to the author\'s website.\\\\n\\\\nAnother thing to consider when creating a website is that in many cases, people are more attracted to parodies of real and famous works of art and literature than those of non-famous and less-known writers. For example, movies such as The Twilight Saga: Eclipse is very popular among fans of the book and it is these fans who go to the trouble of making websites that recreate or re-create certain scenes and even whole chapters of the Twilight Saga from scratch. People looking to find out information about the book may view these sites and leave comments, while people are looking for a simple page that has some fun parodic humor might look to websites such as The Twilight Saga: Eclipse fansite. Therefore, it is important to make sure that the information available on the website is current and relevant to the particular subject matter.\\\\n\\\\nAnother important part of the website is the information available about the website. This is why it is important to put the contact information on the website so that people can send feedback. There are people who look to comment and add content themselves, but this is easier said than done. In order to get the most from a website, the creators need to include a feedback form, where people can leave feedback and suggestions. A website that is properly built will attract people and generate a lot of interest from these people.\\\\n\\\\nI hope you guys enjoy this parody video of LL Cool J got the Rona, a.k.a. coronavirus. In popular parlance, the term can be used to describe an artistic or cultural work that is meant to be both original and funny and to the point.
